    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l26 level3 lfo9;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><span
            style='mso-list:Ignore;'>&#108;<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">上面创建的就是一个简单的虚拟</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">DOM</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">对象</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l33 level1 lfo8;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">虚拟</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">DOM</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">对象最终都会被</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">转换为真实的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">DOM</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l33 level1 lfo8;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:63.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l16 level2 lfo11;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:21.2500pt;mso-para-margin-left:1.9300gd;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

            face="微软雅黑">为什么要拆成模块：随着业务逻辑增加，代码越来越多且复杂。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <h3 style="margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:0.0000pt;mso-list:l0 level3 lfo1;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l58 level1 lfo17;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">理解：用来实现局部功能效果的代码和资源的集合</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(html/css/js/image</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">等等</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l58 level1 lfo17;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">为什么要用组件：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">一个界面的功能更复杂</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l58 level1 lfo17;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">作用：复用编码</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">简化项目编码</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">提高运行效率</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3 style="margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:0.0000pt;mso-list:l0 level3 lfo1;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;
font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.4.3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">模块化</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="text-indent:36.0000pt;line-height:150%;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">当应用的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">都以模块来编写的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">这个应用就是一个模块化的应用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3 style="margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:0.0000pt;mso-list:l0 level3 lfo1;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="text-indent:36.0000pt;line-height:150%;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

            face="微软雅黑">渲染类组件标签的基本流程</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l69 level1 lfo19;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.3. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件三大核心属性</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2: props</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;
mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.3.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;
font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">效果</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;
mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">需求</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">: </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">自定义用来显示一个人员信息的组件</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;layout-grid-mode:char;mso-list:l42 level1 lfo23;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;

font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><i><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;

font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">姓名必须指定，且为字符串类型；</font></span></i><i><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;layout-grid-mode:char;mso-list:l42 level1 lfo23;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;

font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">性别为字符串类型，如果性别没有指定，默认为男</font></span></i><i><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <p class=38 style="margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:36.0000pt;line-height:150%;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:0.2500pt;text-indent:41.7500pt;"><span><span style="position:absolute;z-index:1;margin-left:0.0000px;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.4. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件三大核心属性</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">3: refs</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.4.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">效果</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">需求</font>: <font face="微软雅黑">自定义组件</font><font
            face="Tahoma">, </font><font face="微软雅黑">功能说明如下</font><font face="Tahoma">:</font></span></i><i><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;1. <font face="微软雅黑">点击按钮</font><font face="Tahoma">, </font><font
            face="微软雅黑">提示第一个输入框中的值</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;2. <font face="微软雅黑">当第</font><font face="Tahoma">2</font><font
            face="微软雅黑">个输入框失去焦点时</font><font face="Tahoma">, </font><font
            face="微软雅黑">提示这个输入框中的值</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="line-height:150%;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';line-height:150%;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">效果如下：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';line-height:150%;font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="text-indent:21.0000pt;"><span><img width="99" height="46"

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">.4.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="text-indent:36.0000pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;

            face="微软雅黑">组件内的标签可以定义</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

            face="微软雅黑">属性来标识自己</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal align=justify style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:21.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:1.9100gd;

            face="微软雅黑">字符串形式的</font>ref</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.4.4. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:21.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:1.9100gd;

font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.8200gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l23 level2 lfo29;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">React</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">使用的是自定义</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">合成</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">事件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">而不是使用的原生</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">DOM</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">事件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.8200gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l23 level2 lfo29;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">React</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">中的事件是通过事件委托方式处理的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">委托给组件最外层的元素</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:21.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:1.9100gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l51 level1 lfo28;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">通过</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">event.target</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">得到发生事件的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">DOM</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">元素对象</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.5. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">收集表单数据</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.5.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">效果</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">需求</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

font-size:10.5000pt;">: </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">定义一个包含表单的组件</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

font-size:10.5000pt;">, </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.5.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件的生命周期</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">效果</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">需求</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">:</span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">定义组件实现以下功能：</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;1. </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">让指定的文本做显示</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;/ </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">隐藏的渐变动画</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;2. </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">从完全可见，到彻底消失，耗时</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">2S</span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;3. </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">点击</font>&#8220;不活了&#8221;按钮从界面中卸载组件</span></i><i><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">理解</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo31;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件从创建到死亡它会经历一些特定的阶段。</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo31;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">React</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件中包含一系列勾子函数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">生命周期回调函数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">), </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">会在特定的时刻调用。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo31;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font
            face="微软雅黑">我们在定义组件时，会在特定的生命周期回调函数中，做特定的工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6.3. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">生命周期流程图</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">(</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">旧</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">)</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6.4. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">生命周期流程图</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">(</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">新</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">)</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">2.6.5. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">重要的勾子</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:57.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l76 level1 lfo38;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">：初始化渲染或更新渲染调用</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:57.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l76 level1 lfo38;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">componentDidMount</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">：开启监听</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">创建项目并启动</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:35.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.2700gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:35.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.2700gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:35.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.2700gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:35.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.2700gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">3.1.4. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">功能界面的组件化编码流程（通用）</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">1. </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">拆分组件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">: </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">拆分界面</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">,</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">抽取组件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">2. </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">实现静态组件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">: </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">使用组件实现静态页面效果</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">3. </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">实现动态组件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:21.0000pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">3.1 </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">动态显示初始化数据</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:42.0000pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">3.1.1 </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">数据类型</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:42.0000pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">3.1.2 </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-left:42.0000pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">3.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;

font-size:10.5000pt;">: </span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);
font-style:italic;font-size:10.5000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">组件化实现此功能</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;">todo</span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-ascii-font-family:Tahoma;
mso-hansi-font-family:Tahoma;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);

mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;
font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';color:rgb(127,127,127);font-style:italic;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">4.1.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l77 level1 lfo43;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">轻量级</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">建议使用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l72 level3 lfo44;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">封装</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">4.2. axios</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">);</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
                <p class=MsoNormal align=justify style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;
text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:20.2500pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">});</span><b><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-weight:bold;font-size:15.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
    </table>
    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">4.3. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(121,94,38);font-size:11.0000pt;">catch</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,255);font-size:11.0000pt;">function</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

color:rgb(0,16,128);font-size:11.0000pt;">e</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)&#160;{</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
                <p class=MsoNormal align=justify style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;
text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:20.2500pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,16,128);font-size:11.0000pt;">console</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(121,94,38);font-size:11.0000pt;">log</span><span style="font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

                <p class=MsoNormal align=justify style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;
text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:20.2500pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=41><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.1.1. SPA</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l67 level1 lfo51;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">）。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l67 level1 lfo51;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.1.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l78 level1 lfo52;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-weight:bold;
font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">什么是路由</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-weight:bold;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:63.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l60 level2 lfo53;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">一个路由就是一个映射关系</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(key:value)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:63.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l60 level2 lfo53;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">key</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">为路径</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, value</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">可能是</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">functio</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">n或</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">component</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l78 level1 lfo52;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">路由分类</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-weight:bold;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:63.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l48 level2 lfo54;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">后端路由：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l7 level3 lfo55;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">理解：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">&nbsp;value</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">是</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">function, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">用来处理客户端提交的请求。</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l7 level3 lfo55;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">注册路由：</font> router.get(path, function(req, res))</span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l7 level3 lfo55;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">工作过程：当</font>node接收到一个请求时, 根据请求路径找到匹配的路由, 调用路由中的函数来处理请求, 返回响应数据</span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:63.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l48 level2 lfo54;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">前端路由：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l31 level3 lfo56;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1)<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">浏览器端路由，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">value</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">是</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">component</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">，用于展示页面内容。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l31 level3 lfo56;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">注册路由</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">: &#60;Route path="/test" component={Test}&#62;</span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:84.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;
line-height:150%;mso-list:l31 level3 lfo56;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">工作过程：当浏览器的</font>path变为</span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">/test</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">时</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">当前路由组件就会变为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">T</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">est组件</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.1.3. react-router</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">-dom的理解</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l43 level1 lfo57;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:42.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.2. react-router-dom</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">相关</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">API</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3 style="text-indent:14.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.0000;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:78.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:78.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:78.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:78.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;

    <h3 style="text-indent:21.2500pt;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">5.2.2. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">其它</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:78.5000pt;text-indent:-21.2500pt;
mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo59;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

            href="https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/"><u><span class="20" style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

    <p class=41><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:22.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:22.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">第</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.1. redux</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">理解</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3 style="margin-left:22.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0000gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;

    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;

    <h3 style="margin-left:22.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0000gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">是一个专门用于做</font></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(192,0,0);font-weight:bold;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">JS</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">库</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">不是</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">react</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">插件库</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">等项目中</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">但基本与</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">react</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">配合使用。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=38 style="margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;text-indent:-21.0000pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;mso-list:l59 level1 lfo64;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><font
            face="微软雅黑">作用</font>: 集中式管理react应用中多个组件</span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(192,0,0);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0000pt;
mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">共享</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">的状态。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3 style="margin-left:22.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0000gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.1.3. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">什么情况下需要使用</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">redux</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l3 level1 lfo65;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">某个组件的状态，需要让其他组件可以随时拿到（共享）。</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l3 level1 lfo65;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">一个组件需要改变另一个组件的状态（通信）。</font></span><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.9500pt;mso-para-margin-left:5.2700gd;
text-indent:-21.0000pt;mso-pagination:none;line-height:150%;
mso-list:l3 level1 lfo65;"><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:rgb(0,0,0);
font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">总体原则：能不用就不用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">, </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">如果不用比较吃力才考虑使用。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <h3 style="text-indent:22.0000pt;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.1.4. redux</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">工作流程</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="text-indent:22.0000pt;"><img width="638" height="376"
                                                           src="尚硅谷react全家桶.files/尚硅谷react全家桶9395.png"><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Tahoma;mso-fareast-font-family:微软雅黑;
mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:11.0000pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.2. redux</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">的三个核心概念</font></span></b><b><span
            style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h2>
    <h3 style="margin-left:22.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0000gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.2.1. action</span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h3 style="text-indent:21.0000pt;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';

    <h2><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.8. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">纯函数和高阶函数</font></span></b><b><span

    <h3 style="margin-left:22.0000pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0000gd;"><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">7.8.1. </span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">纯函数</font></span></b><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';
font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></h3>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

font-size:11.0000pt;"><span style='mso-list:Ignore;'>1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">一类特别的函数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">: </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">只要是同样的输入</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">实参</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">，必定得到同样的输出</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">(</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">返回</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;">)</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:10.5000pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style="margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:57.0000pt;text-indent:-21.0000pt;

line-height:150%;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:11.0000pt;"><font face="微软雅黑">不得改写参数数据</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:微软雅黑;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
